            <a aria-label="Briones: Red-zone rules are stacked against Ottawa restaurants" class="article-card__link" href="/news/briones-red-zone-rules-are-stacked-against-ottawa-restaurants">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Briones: Red-zone rules are stacked against Ottawa restaurants">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Briones: Red-zone rules are stacked against Ottawa restaurants
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Retail capacity limits are 75 per cent for supermarkets and other stores that primarily sell groceries;and 50 per cent for other retail. Meanwhile, restaurants can seat only 10 people maximum, regardless of the size of the space.
             </p>
